	<a class="mk-blog-print" onClick="window.print()" href="#" title="Print"><svg  class="mk-svg-icon" data-name="mk-moon-print-3" data-cacheid="icon-589f728840186" style=" height:16px; width: 16px; "  xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M448 288v128h-384v-128h-64v192h512v-192zm-32-256h-320v352h320v-352zm-64 288h-192v-32h192v32zm0-96h-192v-32h192v32zm0-96h-192v-32h192v32z"/></svg></a>

	<div class="essb_links essb_counter_modern_right essb_displayed_top essb_share essb_template_default essb_818017490 print-no" id="essb_displayed_top_818017490" data-essb-postid="2609" data-essb-position="top" data-essb-button-style="button" data-essb-template="default" data-essb-counter-pos="right" data-essb-url="http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/" data-essb-twitter-url="http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/" data-essb-instance="818017490"><ul class="essb_links_list"><li class="essb_item essb_link_pinterest nolightbox"> <a href="http://pinterest.com/pin/create/bookmarklet/?media=http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3703-3.jpg&amp;url=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/&amp;title=Steak+%26+Mushroom+Pot+Pies&amp;description=Steak+%26+Mushroom+Pot+Pies" title="" onclick="essb_window(&#39;http://pinterest.com/pin/create/bookmarklet/?media=http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3703-3.jpg&amp;url=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/&amp;title=Steak+%26+Mushroom+Pot+Pies&amp;description=Steak+%26+Mushroom+Pot+Pies&#39;,&#39;pinterest&#39;,&#39;818017490&#39;); return false; __gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/bookmarklet/?media=http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3703-3.jpg&amp;url=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/&amp;title=Steak+%26+Mushroom+Pot+Pies&amp;description=Steak+%26+Mushroom+Pot+Pies', 'Pin It');" target="_blank" rel="nofollow"><span class="essb_icon"></span><span class="essb_network_name">Pin It</span></a></li><li class="essb_item essb_link_facebook nolightbox"> <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/&t=Steak+%26+Mushroom+Pot+Pies" title="" onclick="essb_window(&#39;http://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/&t=Steak+%26+Mushroom+Pot+Pies&#39;,&#39;facebook&#39;,&#39;818017490&#39;); return false; __gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/&amp;t=Steak+%26+Mushroom+Pot+Pies', 'Facebook');" target="_blank" rel="nofollow"><span class="essb_icon"></span><span class="essb_network_name">Facebook</span></a></li><li class="essb_item essb_link_twitter nolightbox"> <a href="#" title="" onclick="essb_window(&#39;https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=Steak+%26+Mushroom+Pot+Pies&amp;url=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/&amp;counturl=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/&amp;related=SimplyDelishSA&amp;via=SimplyDelishSA&#39;,&#39;twitter&#39;,&#39;818017490&#39;); return false;" target="_blank" rel="nofollow" ><span class="essb_icon"></span><span class="essb_network_name">Twitter</span></a></li><li class="essb_item essb_link_google nolightbox"> <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/" title="" onclick="essb_window(&#39;https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/&#39;,&#39;google&#39;,&#39;818017490&#39;); return false; __gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/', 'Google+');" target="_blank" rel="nofollow"><span class="essb_icon"></span><span class="essb_network_name">Google+</span></a></li><li class="essb_item essb_link_stumbleupon nolightbox"> <a href="http://www.stumbleupon.com/badge/?url=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/" title="" onclick="essb_window(&#39;http://www.stumbleupon.com/badge/?url=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/&#39;,&#39;stumbleupon&#39;,&#39;818017490&#39;); return false; __gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.stumbleupon.com/badge/?url=http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/', 'StumbleUpon');" target="_blank" rel="nofollow"><span class="essb_icon"></span><span class="essb_network_name">StumbleUpon</span></a></li></ul><div class="essb_native_buttons essb_native_after_share"><ul class="essb_links"></ul></div></div><p><a href="http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3695.jpg"><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2611" title="Steak &amp; Mushroom Pot Pie" src="http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3695.jpg" alt="Steak &amp; Mushroom Pot Pie" width="349" height="523" /></a></p>
<p>It&#8217;s the 1st of August. How is it the 1st of August already? I say it every year and every year I feel like it&#8217;s going faster and faster. I sometimes feel overwhelmed at how quickly the years seem to be flying past me. When I was in school I was SO excited when the year&#8217;s would fly past because it would mean our December holidays were upon us, but now, I don&#8217;t know how I&#8217;m going to get everything done I still need to get done this year. But then, this is how I always feel and what doesn&#8217;t get done this year, always seems to get done the next year. It is frightening to think that my babies are turning 3 soon. Three! It feels like yesterday when I was lying on the bed watching them play in my tummy.</p>
<p><a href="http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3692.jpg"><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2610" title="Steak &amp; Mushroom Pot Pie" src="http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3692.jpg" alt="Steak &amp; Mushroom Pot Pie" width="550" height="367" /></a></p>
<p>Anyway, on to the food. As my beautiful hometown, Pretoria, starts warming up during the day and the smell of Jasmine starts filling the air, I know my favourite season, Spring, is just around the corner. There are a lot of things that make me so happy that I have a permanent smile plastered on my face and my toes curl from utter joy, but Spring has to be pretty much at the top of that list. I love the warm days, cool evenings and watching the trees put on their bright green adornments. It means the season of braai-ing (barbecuing), salads and swimming is almost here.</p>
<p><a href="http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3697.jpg"><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2612" title="Steak &amp; Mushroom Pot Pie" src="http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3697.jpg" alt="Steak &amp; Mushroom Pot Pie" width="349" height="523" /></a></p>
<p>But I still need comfort food every now and then and before my second favourite season, Winter, goes away for a while, I need to soak up as much comfort food as I can. After curries, warm pies are my absolute favourite Winter food and these pot pies are sheer perfection. The steak and mushroom stew is rich, meaty and flavourful. If you don&#8217;t want to use stewing steak (or chuck steak), you can use beef shin, oxtail or any other stewing beef you happen to have around. Just make sure you remove any bones before putting the mixture into the pie. Nothing worse than munching through a pie only to almost break your tooth on a bone half way through.</p>
<p><a href="http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3703.jpg"><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2613" title="Steak &amp; Mushroom Pot Pie" src="http://simply-delicious-food.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/08/MG_3703.jpg" alt="Steak &amp; Mushroom Pot Pie" width="349" height="523" /></a></p>
<p>These pies don&#8217;t have pastry at the bottom (hence the name: Pot pie) but if you, like me, can never have enough pastry, feel free to put more pastry at the bottom of the baking dish. You can also make mini-pies like I did with my <a href="http://simply-delicious-food.com/2011/06/27/beef-shin-pie/">Beef Shin Pie</a>. I served our pot pies with steamed vegetables but I think this would go so well with maple glazed carrots or a simple salad as well.</p>
<p><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Makes 4-6 pot pies</span></p>
<p>1.5kg stewing beef (I used chuck steak cut into chunks, bone removed)<br />
1 large onion, diced<br />
3 carrots, diced<br />
2 celery sticks, diced<br />
250g mushrooms, sliced<br />
2 cloves garlic, crushed<br />
2 tsp smoked paprika<br />
1 tsp each dried thyme, dried rosemary and dried oregano (I like the earthiness of the dried herbs)<br />
2 bay leaves<br />
500ml (2 cups) strong beef stock (alternatively add a heaped tbsp bovril to 500ml water)<br />
1 tbsp cornflour mixed with 50ml milk<br />
salt &amp; pepper to taste<br />
1 roll ready-made puff pastry, rolled out slightly<br />
1 egg, beaten</p>
<ul>
<li>For the filling, brown the beef in a large pot. Remove and set aside.</li>
<li>In the same pot, fry the onion, carrots and celery sticks until soft and fragrant (about 10 minutes).</li>
<li>Add the mushrooms and garlic and fry for 5 minutes before adding the paprika and herbs.</li>
<li>Pour in the stock and add the browned beef back into the pot. Stir to combine everything and reduce the heat. Cover the pot and allow the stew to simmer gently for 1 1/2 &#8211; 2 hours.</li>
<li>When the meat is really tender (when you press a piece with a spoon it should break apart), turn the heat up and pour in the cornflour mixture. Allow the sauce to simmer rapidly and thicken for about 10 minutes.</li>
<li>Pre-heat the oven to 180°c.</li>
<li>Divide the beef and mushroom filling between 4-6 oven-proof dishes (depending on size).</li>
<li>Cut the pastry into squares big enough to cover the dishes, it doesn&#8217;t have to be perfect. Brush the rim of the dishes with some of the beaten egg then place the pastry on top and pinch the pastry onto the rim.</li>
<li>Cut 2 slits into each pie to allow the steam to escape and brush with the rest of the beaten egg.</li>
<li>Place in the oven and bake for 25-30 minutes until the pastry is cooked through and golden brown.</li>
<li>Remove and serve with vegetables of your choice.</li>
</ul>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

			<div class="gravatar"><img alt='' src='http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/fa4ff65c7797adf6c0ec6b4d849de2a4?s=45&#038;r=g' srcset='http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/fa4ff65c7797adf6c0ec6b4d849de2a4?s=90&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-45 photo' height='45' width='45' /></div>
			<div class="comment-meta">
					<span class="comment-author" itemprop="creator" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" rel="external nofollow" >brandyspeonk</span>					
                                        <time class="comment-time" itemprop="datePublished" itemscope="itemscope" datetime="2011-08-01T07:50:02+00:00" >February 17, 2014</time>
			</div>
			<span class="comment-reply">
					<a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='http://simply-delicious-food.com/steak-mushroom-pot-pies/?replytocom=92516#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-92516", "92516", "respond", "2609" )' aria-label='Reply to brandyspeonk'>Reply</a>			</span>
			<div class="clearboth"></div>
			<div class="comment-content" itemprop="text" >
					<p>Jamie and Alida, I would like to ad a suggestion. I would leave off the puff pastry before I freeze it. Since I&#8217;m sure we&#8217;re all using frozen puff pastry, it&#8217;s just a defrost the filling and the pastry and it&#8217;s done. You can freeze the filling in the pots you intend to use to cook in if you can or just freeze in one container and when defrosted put in the pots you&#8217;re going to use and put the pastry on top. I just think the dough gets a bit gummy after it&#8217;s defrosted and refrozen. That&#8217;s my experience with the pastry and it doesn&#8217;t ad any extra work. Can&#8217;t wait to make this tomorrow Alida!!</p>

				<div class="clearboth"></div>
			</div>

		       
		</div>

        // Run this very early after DOM is ready
        (function ($) {
            // Prevent browser native behaviour of jumping to anchor
            // while preserving support for current links (shared across net or internally on page)
            var loc = window.location,
                hash = loc.hash;

            // Detect hashlink and change it's name with !loading appendix
            if(hash.length && hash.substring(1).length) {
                var $topLevelSections = $('.vc_row, .mk-main-wrapper-holder, .mk-page-section, #comments');
                var $section = $topLevelSections.filter( '#' + hash.substring(1) );
                // We smooth scroll only to page section and rows where we define our anchors.
                // This should prevent conflict with third party plugins relying on hash
                if( ! $section.length )  return;
                // Mutate hash for some good reason - crazy jumps of browser. We want really smooth scroll on load
                // Discard loading state if it already exists in url (multiple refresh)
                hash = hash.replace( '!loading', '' );
                var newUrl = hash + '!loading';
                loc.hash = newUrl;
            }
        }(jQuery));
    </script>
